Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not in place, apply strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the thigh, until it stabilizes.
de la dislocation dou talon	From the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are never fully set and always partially dislocated, both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen and tries to move before it dislocates: the reset should be quick, and one must gently extend it with their hands when it is only slightly moved.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is dislocated completely, one must have the patient lie straight and hold the leg up by lifting their ankle; then pull the foot towards your right hand, and then to your left twice, then lift it high, and firmly bend the leg upwards; repeat this two times as we have said, while pulling and moving the leg. If it returns, it is well; if not, restart the process, for it will return; and if it cannot return like this, one must remove the patient on their back to the ground, firmly plant the leg between their thighs in the earth, and tie strips tightly around them so as not to pinch the ankle. Then, have the helpers cut away their thighs, and with another helper extend the foot towards their hands or a stake, which they bind to the neck of the leg; then equally stretch each helper and place the stake firmly between the thighs for holding the leg when it is extended; finally, make the dislocation equal on both hands, and have another helper cut the healthy leg right after the knee, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it reaches the point, apply the plaster and bandage over it, hold it firm, tie the leg to the joint, and guard the nerves that are behind the ankle, ensuring the bandage is not too tight; then leave it for two or three days. If the bandage loosens, loosen it; then remove the bandages on the third day or the fourth, and guide the patient for three more days; and if it progresses beyond this stage, there is no guarantee that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the abscesses come out, then it is necessary that you soothe them, as we have said elsewhere, until they are clean.
des dois	do not specify
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both shoulders are dislocated, if they fit beautifully to extend with work, and this is a minor matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in no bone of the back or leg joint, you should make the patient lie on their full length or flat on a table completely straight, and place your foot where it opens from these joints, then press with your foot firmly until they recover. And when it's even and there is nothing opening, put under the heel of the foot a board for two shoulders, then hold them firmly in place, and let them rest for three days, then release; and make them rest until they are well again.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	regarding wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When injury accompanies dislocation, and you wish to restore it, many times the patient dies: if you are not presumptuous in your treatment, if you are skilled in the art and have used it for a long time, and if you are kind and merciful but not hasty; then do not be bold; start by treating with calming abscess removal methods, leave the patient to God's mercy if you do not see hope of recovery; and when you do see hope, immediately reset the limb in place, as if removing the abscesses is complete; and when the limb is in place, apply calming abscess removal techniques, treat the wound appropriately with dried ointments; and if due to dislocation there are fractures, and small bone fragments are exposed, set them, and do what we have said about simple diseases; and refrain from entering paths of fear as I instructed, because this is your Creator's will, and for the wisdom you arm yourself and your body with.
Amen	Amen
